148→GrpcMuxImpl::~GrpcMuxImpl() { AllMuxes::get().erase(this); }\n   149→\n   150→void GrpcMuxImpl::shutdownAll() { AllMuxes::get().shutdownAll(); }\n   151→\n   152→void GrpcMuxImpl::onDynamicContextUpdate(absl::string_view resource_type_url) {\n   153→  auto api_state = api_state_.find(resource_type_url);\n   154→  if (api_state == api_state_.end()) {\n   155→    return;\n   156→  }\n   157→  api_state->second->must_send_node_ = true;\n   158→  queueDiscoveryRequest(resource_type_url);\n   159→}\n   160→\n   161→void GrpcMuxImpl::start() {\n   162→  ASSERT(!started_);\n   163→  if (started_) {\n   164→    return;\n   165→  }\n   166→  started_ = true;\n   167→  grpc_stream_->establishNewStream();\n   168→}\n   169→\n   170→void GrpcMuxImpl::sendDiscoveryRequest(absl::string_view type_url) {\n   171→  if (shutdown_) {\n   172→    return;\n   173→  }\n   174→\n   175→  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   176→  auto& request = api_state.request_;\n   177→  request.mutable_resource_names()->Clear();\n   178→\n   179→  // Maintain a set to avoid dupes.\n   180→  absl::node_hash_set<std::string> resources;\n   181→  for (const auto* watch : api_state.watches_) {\n   182→    for (const std::string& resource : watch->resources_) {\n   183→      if (!resources.contains(resource)) {\n   184→        resources.emplace(resource);\n   185→        request.add_resource_names(resource);\n   186→      }\n   187→    }\n   188→  }\n   189→\n   190→  if (api_state.must_send_node_ || !skip_subsequent_node_ || first_stream_request_) {\n   191→    // Node may have been cleared during a previous request.\n   192→    request.mutable_node()->CopyFrom(local_info_.node());\n   193→    api_state.must_send_node_ = false;\n   194→  } else {\n   195→    request.clear_node();\n   196→  }\n   197→  ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"Sending DiscoveryRequest for {}: {}\", type_url, request.ShortDebugString());\n   198→  grpc_stream_->sendMessage(request);\n   199→  first_stream_request_ = false;\n   200→\n   201→  // clear error_detail after the request is sent if it exists.\n   202→  if (apiStateFor(type_url).request_.has_error_detail()) {\n   203→    apiStateFor(type_url).request_.clear_error_detail();\n   204→  }\n   205→}\n   206→\n   207→void GrpcMuxImpl::clearNonce() {\n   208→  // Iterate over all api_states (for each type_url), and clear its nonce.\n   209→  for (auto& [type_url, api_state] : api_state_) {\n   210→    if (api_state) {\n   211→      api_state->request_.clear_response_nonce();\n   212→    }\n   213→  }\n   214→}\n   215→\n   216→void GrpcMuxImpl::loadConfigFromDelegate(const std::string& type_url,\n   217→                                         const absl::flat_hash_set<std::string>& resource_names) {\n   218→  if (!xds_resources_delegate_.has_value()) {\n   219→    return;\n   220→  }\n   221→  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   222→  if (api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n   223→    // No watches, so exit without loading config from storage.\n   224→    return;\n   225→  }\n   226→\n   227→  const XdsConfigSourceId source_id{target_xds_authority_, type_url};\n   228→  TRY_ASSERT_MAIN_THREAD {\n   229→    std::vector<envoy::service::discovery::v3::Resource> resources =\n   230→        xds_resources_delegate_->getResources(source_id, resource_names);\n   231→    if (resources.empty()) {\n   232→      // There are no persisted resources, so nothing to process.\n   233→      return;\n   234→    }\n   235→\n   236→    std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr> decoded_resources;\n   237→    OpaqueResourceDecoder& resource_decoder = *api_state.watches_.front()->resource_decoder_;\n   238→    std::string version_info;\n   239→    for (const auto& resource : resources) {\n   240→      if (version_info.empty()) {\n   241→        version_info = resource.version();\n   242→      } else {\n   243→        ASSERT(resource.version() == version_info);\n   244→      }\n   245→\n   246→      TRY_ASSERT_MAIN_THREAD {\n   247→        decoded_resources.emplace_back(\n   248→            std::make_unique<DecodedResourceImpl>(resource_decoder, resource));\n   249→      }\n   250→      END_TRY\n   251→      CATCH(const EnvoyException& e,\n   252→            { xds_resources_delegate_->onResourceLoadFailed(source_id, resource.name(), e); });\n   253→    }\n   254→\n   255→    processDiscoveryResources(decoded_resources, api_state, type_url, version_info,\n   256→                              /*call_delegate=*/false);\n   257→  }\n   258→  END_TRY\n   259→  CATCH(const EnvoyException& e, {\n   260→    // TODO(abeyad): do something else here?\n   261→    ENVOY_LOG_MISC(warn, \"Failed to load config from delegate for {}: {}\", source_id.toKey(),\n   262→                   e.what());\n   263→  });\n   264→}\n   265→\n   266→GrpcMuxWatchPtr GrpcMuxImpl::addWatch(const std::string& type_url,\n   267→                                      const absl::flat_hash_set<std::string>& resources,\n   268→                                      SubscriptionCallbacks& callbacks,\n   269→                                      OpaqueResourceDecoderSharedPtr resource_decoder,\n   270→                                      const SubscriptionOptions& options) {\n   271→  // Resource cache is only used for EDS resources.\n   272→  EdsResourcesCacheOptRef resources_cache{absl::nullopt};\n   273→  if (eds_resources_cache_ &&\n   274→      (type_url == Config::getTypeUrl<envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment>())) {\n   275→    resources_cache = makeOptRefFromPtr(eds_resources_cache_.get());\n   276→  }\n   277→  auto watch = std::make_unique<GrpcMuxWatchImpl>(resources, callbacks, resource_decoder, type_url,\n   278→                                                  *this, options, local_info_, resources_cache);\n   279→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"gRPC mux addWatch for \" + type_url);\n   280→\n   281→  // Lazily kick off the requests based on first subscription. This has the\n   282→  // convenient side-effect that we order messages on the channel based on\n   283→  // Envoy's internal dependency ordering.\n   284→  // TODO(gsagula): move TokenBucketImpl params to a config.\n   285→  if (!apiStateFor(type_url).subscribed_) {\n   286→    apiStateFor(type_url).request_.set_type_url(type_url);\n   287→    apiStateFor(type_url).request_.mutable_node()->MergeFrom(local_info_.node());\n   288→    apiStateFor(type_url).subscribed_ = true;\n   289→    subscriptions_.emplace_back(type_url);\n   290→  }\n   291→\n   292→  // This will send an updated request on each subscription.\n   293→  // TODO(htuch): For RDS/EDS, this will generate a new DiscoveryRequest on each resource we added.\n   294→  // Consider in the future adding some kind of collation/batching during CDS/LDS updates so that we\n   295→  // only send a single RDS/EDS update after the CDS/LDS update.\n   296→  queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n   297→\n   298→  return watch;\n   299→}\n   300→\n   301→absl::Status\n   302→GrpcMuxImpl::updateMuxSource(Grpc::RawAsyncClientSharedPtr&& primary_async_client,\n   303→                             Grpc::RawAsyncClientSharedPtr&& failover_async_client,\n   304→                             Stats::Scope& scope, BackOffStrategyPtr&& backoff_strategy,\n   305→                             const envoy::config::core::v3::ApiConfigSource& ads_config_source) {\n   306→  // Process the rate limit settings.\n   307→  absl::StatusOr<RateLimitSettings> rate_limit_settings_or_error =\n   308→      Utility::parseRateLimitSettings(ads_config_source);\n   309→  RETURN_IF_NOT_OK_REF(rate_limit_settings_or_error.status());\n   310→\n   311→  const Protobuf::MethodDescriptor& service_method =\n   312→      *Protobuf::DescriptorPool::generated_pool()->FindMethodByName(\n   313→          \"envoy.service.discovery.v3.AggregatedDiscoveryService.StreamAggregatedResources\");\n   314→\n   315→  // Disconnect from current xDS servers.\n   316→  ENVOY_LOG_MISC(info, \"Replacing xDS gRPC mux source\");\n   317→  grpc_stream_->closeStream();\n   318→  grpc_stream_ = createGrpcStreamObject(std::move(primary_async_client),\n   319→                                        std::move(failover_async_client), service_method, scope,\n   320→                                        std::move(backoff_strategy), *rate_limit_settings_or_error);\n   321→  // No need to update the config_validators_ as they may contain some state\n   322→  // that needs to be kept across different GrpcMux objects.\n   323→\n   324→  // Start the subscriptions over the grpc_stream.\n   325→  grpc_stream_->establishNewStream();\n   326→\n   327→  return absl::OkStatus();\n   328→}\n   329→\n   330→ScopedResume GrpcMuxImpl::pause(const std::string& type_url) {\n   331→  return pause(std::vector<std::string>{type_url});\n   332→}\n   333→\n   334→ScopedResume GrpcMuxImpl::pause(const std::vector<std::string> type_urls) {\n   335→  for (const auto& type_url : type_urls) {\n   336→    ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   337→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Pausing discovery requests for {} (previous count {})\", type_url,\n   338→              api_state.pauses_);\n   339→    ++api_state.pauses_;\n   340→  }\n   341→  return std::make_unique<Cleanup>([this, type_urls]() {\n   342→    for (const auto& type_url : type_urls) {\n   343→      ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   344→      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Decreasing pause count on discovery requests for {} (previous count {})\",\n   345→                type_url, api_state.pauses_);\n   346→      ASSERT(api_state.paused());\n   347→\n   348→      if (--api_state.pauses_ == 0 && api_state.pending_ && api_state.subscribed_) {\n   349→        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Resuming discovery requests for {}\", type_url);\n   350→        queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n   351→        api_state.pending_ = false;\n   352→      }\n   353→    }\n   354→  });\n   355→}\n   356→\n   357→void GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse(\n   358→    std::unique_ptr<envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse>&& message,\n   359→    ControlPlaneStats& control_plane_stats) {\n   360→  const std::string type_url = message->type_url();\n   361→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Received gRPC message for {} at version {}\", type_url, message->version_info());\n   362→\n   363→  if (api_state_.count(type_url) == 0) {\n   364→    // TODO(yuval-k): This should never happen. consider dropping the stream as this is a\n   365→    // protocol violation\n   366→    ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Ignoring the message for type URL {} as it has no current subscribers.\",\n   367→              type_url);\n   368→    return;\n   369→  }\n   370→\n   371→  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   372→\n   373→  if (message->has_control_plane()) {\n   374→    control_plane_stats.identifier_.set(message->control_plane().identifier());\n   375→\n   376→    if (message->control_plane().identifier() != api_state.control_plane_identifier_) {\n   377→      api_state.control_plane_identifier_ = message->control_plane().identifier();\n   378→      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Receiving gRPC updates for {} from {}\", type_url,\n   379→                api_state.control_plane_identifier_);\n   380→    }\n   381→  }\n   382→\n   383→  if (api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n   384→    // update the nonce as we are processing this response.\n   385→    api_state.request_.set_response_nonce(message->nonce());\n   386→    if (message->resources().empty()) {\n   387→      // No watches and no resources. This can happen when envoy unregisters from a\n   388→      // resource that's removed from the server as well. For example, a deleted cluster\n   389→      // triggers un-watching the ClusterLoadAssignment watch, and at the same time the\n   390→      // xDS server sends an empty list of ClusterLoadAssignment resources. we'll accept\n   391→      // this update. no need to send a discovery request, as we don't watch for anything.\n   392→      api_state.request_.set_version_info(message->version_info());\n   393→    } else {\n   394→      // No watches and we have resources - this should not happen. send a NACK (by not\n   395→      // updating the version).\n   396→      ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Ignoring unwatched type URL {}\", type_url);\n   397→      queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n   398→    }\n   399→    return;\n   400→  }\n   401→  ScopedResume same_type_resume;\n   402→  // We pause updates of the same type. This is necessary for SotW and GrpcMuxImpl, since unlike\n   403→  // delta and NewGRpcMuxImpl, independent watch additions/removals trigger updates regardless of\n   404→  // the delta state. The proper fix for this is to converge these implementations,\n   405→  // see https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/11477.\n   406→  same_type_resume = pause(type_url);\n   407→  TRY_ASSERT_MAIN_THREAD {\n   408→    std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr> resources;\n   409→    OpaqueResourceDecoder& resource_decoder = *api_state.watches_.front()->resource_decoder_;\n   410→\n   411→    for (const auto& resource : message->resources()) {\n   412→      // TODO(snowp): Check the underlying type when the resource is a Resource.\n   413→      if (!resource.Is<envoy::service::discovery::v3::Resource>() &&\n   414→          type_url != resource.type_url()) {\n   415→        throwEnvoyExceptionOrPanic(\n   416→            fmt::format(\"{} does not match the message-wide type URL {} in DiscoveryResponse {}\",\n   417→                        resource.type_url(), type_url, message->DebugString()));\n   418→      }\n   419→\n   420→      auto decoded_resource = THROW_OR_RETURN_VALUE(\n   421→          DecodedResourceImpl::fromResource(resource_decoder, resource, message->version_info()),\n   422→          DecodedResourceImplPtr);\n   423→\n   424→      if (!isHeartbeatResource(type_url, *decoded_resource)) {\n   425→        resources.emplace_back(std::move(decoded_resource));\n   426→      }\n   427→    }\n   428→\n   429→    processDiscoveryResources(resources, api_state, type_url, message->version_info(),\n   430→                              /*call_delegate=*/true);\n   431→\n   432→    // Processing point when resources are successfully ingested.\n   433→    if (xds_config_tracker_.has_value()) {\n   434→      xds_config_tracker_->onConfigAccepted(type_url, resources);\n   435→    }\n   436→  }\n   437→  END_TRY\n   438→  CATCH(const EnvoyException& e, {\n   439→    for (auto watch : api_state.watches_) {\n   440→      watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdateFailed(\n   441→          Envoy::Config::ConfigUpdateFailureReason::UpdateRejected, &e);\n   442→    }\n   443→    ::google::rpc::Status* error_detail = api_state.request_.mutable_error_detail();\n   444→    error_detail->set_code(Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Internal);\n   445→    error_detail->set_message(Config::Utility::truncateGrpcStatusMessage(e.what()));\n   446→\n   447→    // Processing point when there is any exception during the parse and ingestion process.\n   448→    if (xds_config_tracker_.has_value()) {\n   449→      xds_config_tracker_->onConfigRejected(*message, error_detail->message());\n   450→    }\n   451→  });\n   452→  api_state.previously_fetched_data_ = true;\n   453→  api_state.request_.set_response_nonce(message->nonce());\n   454→  ASSERT(api_state.paused());\n   455→  queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n   456→}\n   457→\n   458→void GrpcMuxImpl::processDiscoveryResources(const std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr>& resources,\n   459→                                            ApiState& api_state, const std::string& type_url,\n   460→                                            const std::string& version_info,\n   461→                                            const bool call_delegate) {\n   462→  ASSERT_IS_MAIN_OR_TEST_THREAD();\n   463→  // To avoid O(n^2) explosion (e.g. when we have 1000s of EDS watches), we\n   464→  // build a map here from resource name to resource and then walk watches_.\n   465→  // We have to walk all watches (and need an efficient map as a result) to\n   466→  // ensure we deliver empty config updates when a resource is dropped. We make the map ordered\n   467→  // for test determinism.\n   468→  absl::btree_map<std::string, DecodedResourceRef> resource_ref_map;\n   469→  std::vector<DecodedResourceRef> all_resource_refs;\n   470→\n   471→  const auto scoped_ttl_update = api_state.ttl_.scopedTtlUpdate();\n   472→\n   473→  for (const auto& resource : resources) {\n   474→    if (resource->ttl()) {\n   475→      api_state.ttl_.add(*resource->ttl(), resource->name());\n   476→    } else {\n   477→      api_state.ttl_.clear(resource->name());\n   478→    }\n   479→\n   480→    all_resource_refs.emplace_back(*resource);\n   481→    if (XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource->name())) {\n   482→      // Sort the context params of an xdstp resource, so we can compare them easily.\n   483→      auto resource_or_error = XdsResourceIdentifier::decodeUrn(resource->name());\n   484→      THROW_IF_NOT_OK_REF(resource_or_error.status());\n   485→      xds::core::v3::ResourceName xdstp_resource = resource_or_error.value();\n   486→      XdsResourceIdentifier::EncodeOptions options;\n   487→      options.sort_context_params_ = true;\n   488→      resource_ref_map.emplace(XdsResourceIdentifier::encodeUrn(xdstp_resource, options),\n   489→                               *resource);\n   490→    } else {\n   491→      resource_ref_map.emplace(resource->name(), *resource);\n   492→    }\n   493→  }\n   494→\n   495→  // Execute external config validators if there are any watches.\n   496→  if (!api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n   497→    config_validators_->executeValidators(type_url, resources);\n   498→  }\n   499→\n   500→  for (auto watch : api_state.watches_) {\n   501→    // onConfigUpdate should be called in all cases for single watch xDS (Cluster and\n   502→    // Listener) even if the message does not have resources so that update_empty stat\n   503→    // is properly incremented and state-of-the-world semantics are maintained.\n   504→    if (watch->resources_.empty()) {\n   505→      THROW_IF_NOT_OK(watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdate(all_resource_refs, version_info));\n   506→      continue;\n   507→    }\n   508→    std::vector<DecodedResourceRef> found_resources;\n   509→    for (const auto& watched_resource_name : watch->resources_) {\n   510→      // Look for a singleton subscription.\n   511→      auto it = resource_ref_map.find(watched_resource_name);\n   512→      if (it != resource_ref_map.end()) {\n   513→        found_resources.emplace_back(it->second);\n   514→      } else if (isXdsTpWildcard(watched_resource_name)) {\n   515→        // See if the resources match the xdstp wildcard subscription.\n   516→        // Note: although it is unlikely that Envoy will need to support a resource that is mapped\n   517→        // to both a singleton and collection watch, this code still supports this use case.\n   518→        // TODO(abeyad): This could be made more efficient, e.g. by pre-computing and having a map\n   519→        // entry for each wildcard watch.\n   520→        for (const auto& resource_ref_it : resource_ref_map) {\n   521→          if (XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource_ref_it.first) &&\n   522→              convertToWildcard(resource_ref_it.first) == watched_resource_name) {\n   523→            found_resources.emplace_back(resource_ref_it.second);\n   524→          }\n   525→        }\n   526→      }\n   527→    }\n   528→\n   529→    // onConfigUpdate should be called only on watches(clusters/listeners) that have\n   530→    // updates in the message for EDS/RDS.\n   531→    if (!found_resources.empty()) {\n   532→      THROW_IF_NOT_OK(watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdate(found_resources, version_info));\n   533→      // Resource cache is only used for EDS resources.\n   534→      if (eds_resources_cache_ &&\n   535→          (type_url == Config::getTypeUrl<envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment>())) {\n   536→        for (const auto& resource : found_resources) {\n   537→          const envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment& cluster_load_assignment =\n   538→              dynamic_cast<const envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment&>(\n   539→                  resource.get().resource());\n   540→          eds_resources_cache_->setResource(resource.get().name(), cluster_load_assignment);\n   541→        }\n   542→        // No need to remove resources from the cache, as currently only non-collection\n   543→        // subscriptions are supported, and these resources are removed in the call\n   544→        // to updateWatchInterest().\n   545→      }\n   546→    }\n   547→  }\n   548→\n   549→  // All config updates have been applied without throwing an exception, so we'll call the xDS\n   550→  // resources delegate, if any.\n   551→  if (call_delegate && xds_resources_delegate_.has_value()) {\n   552→    xds_resources_delegate_->onConfigUpdated(XdsConfigSourceId{target_xds_authority_, type_url},\n   553→                                             all_resource_refs);\n   554→  }\n   555→\n   556→  // TODO(mattklein123): In the future if we start tracking per-resource versions, we\n   557→  // would do that tracking here.\n   558→  api_state.request_.set_version_info(version_info);\n   559→  Memory::Utils::tryShrinkHeap();\n   560→}\n   561→\n   562→void GrpcMuxImpl::onWriteable() { drainRequests(); }\n   563→\n   564→void GrpcMuxImpl::onStreamEstablished() {\n   565→  first_stream_request_ = true;\n   566→  grpc_stream_->maybeUpdateQueueSizeStat(0);\n   567→  clearNonce();\n   568→  request_queue_ = std::make_unique<std::queue<std::string>>();\n   569→  for (const auto& type_url : subscriptions_) {\n   570→    queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n   571→  }\n   572→}\n   573→\n   574→void GrpcMuxImpl::onEstablishmentFailure(bool) {\n   575→  for (const auto& api_state : api_state_) {\n   576→    for (auto watch : api_state.second->watches_) {\n   577→      watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdateFailed(\n   578→          Envoy::Config::ConfigUpdateFailureReason::ConnectionFailure, nullptr);\n   579→    }\n   580→    if (!api_state.second->previously_fetched_data_) {\n   581→      // On the initialization of the gRPC mux, if connection to the xDS server fails, load the\n   582→      // persisted config, if available. The locally persisted config will be used until\n   583→      // connectivity is established with the xDS server.\n   584→      loadConfigFromDelegate(\n   585→          /*type_url=*/api_state.first,\n   586→          absl::flat_hash_set<std::string>{api_state.second->request_.resource_names().begin(),\n   587→                                           api_state.second->request_.resource_names().end()});\n   588→      api_state.second->previously_fetched_data_ = true;\n   589→    }\n   590→  }\n   591→}\n   592→\n   593→void GrpcMuxImpl::queueDiscoveryRequest(absl::string_view queue_item) {\n   594→  if (!grpc_stream_->grpcStreamAvailable()) {\n   595→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"No stream available to queueDiscoveryRequest for {}\", queue_item);\n   596→    return; // Drop this request; the reconnect will enqueue a new one.\n   597→  }\n   598→  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(queue_item);\n   599→  if (api_state.paused()) {\n   600→    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"API {} paused during queueDiscoveryRequest(), setting pending.\", queue_item);\n   601→    api_state.pending_ = true;\n   602→    return; // Drop apiStateFor(type_url);\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Pausing discovery requests for {} (previous count {})\", type_url,\n              api_state.pauses_);\n    ++api_state.pauses_;\n  }\n  return std::make_unique<Cleanup>([this, type_urls]() {\n    for (const auto& type_url : type_urls) {\n      ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Decreasing pause count on discovery requests for {} (previous count {})\",\n                type_url, api_state.pauses_);\n      ASSERT(api_state.paused());\n\n      if (--api_state.pauses_ == 0 && api_state.pending_ && api_state.subscribed_) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Resuming discovery requests for {}\", type_url);\n        queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n        api_state.pending_ = false;\n      }\n    }\n  });\n}\n\nvoid GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse(\n    std::unique_ptr<envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse>&& message,\n    ControlPlaneStats& control_plane_stats) {\n  const std::string type_url = message->type_url();\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Received gRPC message for {} at version {}\", type_url, message->version_info());\n\n  if (api_state_.count(type_url) == 0) {\n    // TODO(yuval-k): This should never happen. consider dropping the stream as this is a\n    // protocol violation\n    ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Ignoring the message for type URL {} as it has no current subscribers.\",\n              type_url);\n    return;\n  }\n\n  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n\n  if (message->has_control_plane()) {\n    control_plane_stats.identifier_.set(message->control_plane().identifier());\n\n    if (message->control_plane().identifier() != api_state.control_plane_identifier_) {\n      api_state.control_plane_identifier_ = message->control_plane().identifier();\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Receiving gRPC updates for {} from {}\", type_url,\n                api_state.control_plane_identifier_);\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n    // update the nonce as we are processing this response.\n    api_state.request_.set_response_nonce(message->nonce());\n    if (message->resources().empty()) {\n      // No watches and no resources. This can happen when envoy unregisters from a\n      // resource that's removed from the server as well. For example, a deleted cluster\n      // triggers un-watching the ClusterLoadAssignment watch, and at the same time the\n      // xDS server sends an empty list of ClusterLoadAssignment resources. we'll accept\n      // this update. no need to send a discovery request, as we don't watch for anything.\n      api_state.request_.set_version_info(message->version_info());\n    } else {\n      // No watches and we have resources - this should not happen. send a NACK (by not\n      // updating the version).\n      ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Ignoring unwatched type URL {}\", type_url);\n      queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n    }\n    return;\n  }\n  ScopedResume same_type_resume;\n  // We pause updates of the same type. This is necessary for SotW and GrpcMuxImpl, since unlike\n  // delta and NewGRpcMuxImpl, independent watch additions/removals trigger updates regardless of\n  // the delta state. The proper fix for this is to converge these implementations,\n  // see https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/11477.\n  same_type_resume = pause(type_url);\n  TRY_ASSERT_MAIN_THREAD {\n    std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr> resources;\n    OpaqueResourceDecoder& resource_decoder = *api_state.watches_.front()->resource_decoder_;\n\n    for (const auto& resource : message->resources()) {\n      // TODO(snowp): Check the underlying type when the resource is a Resource.\n      if (!resource.Is<envoy::service::discovery::v3::Resource>() &&\n          type_url != resource.type_url()) {\n        throwEnvoyExceptionOrPanic(\n            fmt::format(\"{} does not match the message-wide type URL {} in DiscoveryResponse {}\",\n                        resource.type_url(), type_url, message->DebugString()));\n      }\n\n      auto decoded_resource = THROW_OR_RETURN_VALUE(\n          DecodedResourceImpl::fromResource(resource_decoder, resource, message->version_info()),\n          DecodedResourceImplPtr);\n\n      if (!isHeartbeatResource(type_url, *decoded_resource)) {\n        resources.emplace_back(std::move(decoded_resource));\n      }\n    }\n\n    processDiscoveryResources(resources, api_state, type_url, message->version_info(),\n                              /*call_delegate=*/true);\n\n    // Processing point when resources are successfully ingested.\n    if (xds_config_tracker_.has_value()) {\n      xds_config_tracker_->onConfigAccepted(type_url, resources);\n    }\n  }\n  END_TRY\n  CATCH(const EnvoyException& e, {\n    for (auto watch : api_state.watches_) {\n      watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdateFailed(\n          Envoy::Config::ConfigUpdateFailureReason::UpdateRejected, &e);\n    }\n    ::google::rpc::Status* error_detail = api_state.request_.mutable_error_detail();\n    error_detail->set_code(Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Internal);\n    error_detail->set_message(Config::Utility::truncateGrpcStatusMessage(e.what()));\n\n    // Processing point when there is any exception during the parse and ingestion process.\n    if (xds_config_tracker_.has_value()) {\n      xds_config_tracker_->onConfigRejected(*message, error_detail->message());\n    }\n  });\n  api_state.previously_fetched_data_ = true;\n  api_state.request_.set_response_nonce(message->nonce());\n  ASSERT(api_state.paused());\n  queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n}\n\nvoid GrpcMuxImpl::processDiscoveryResources(const std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr>& resources,\n                                            ApiState& api_state, const std::string& type_url,\n                                            const std::string& version_info,\n                                            const bool call_delegate) {\n  ASSERT_IS_MAIN_OR_TEST_THREAD();\n  // To avoid O(n^2) explosion (e.g. when we have 1000s of EDS watches), we\n  // build a map here from resource name to resource and then walk watches_.\n  // We have to walk all watches (and need an efficient map as a result) to\n  // ensure we deliver empty config updates when a resource is dropped. We make the map ordered\n  // for test determinism.\n  absl::btree_map<std::string, DecodedResourceRef> resource_ref_map;\n  std::vector<DecodedResourceRef> all_resource_refs;\n\n  const auto scoped_ttl_update = api_state.ttl_.scopedTtlUpdate();\n\n  for (const auto& resource : resources) {\n    if (resource->ttl()) {\n      api_state.ttl_.add(*resource->ttl(), resource->name());\n    } else {\n      api_state.ttl_.clear(resource->name());\n    }\n\n    all_resource_refs.emplace_back(*resource);\n    if (XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource->name())) {\n      // Sort the context params of an xdstp resource, so we can compare them easily.\n      auto resource_or_error = XdsResourceIdentifier::decodeUrn(resource->name());\n      THROW_IF_NOT_OK_REF(resource_or_error.status());\n      xds::core::v3::ResourceName xdstp_resource = resource_or_error.value();\n      XdsResourceIdentifier::EncodeOptions options;\n      options.sort_context_params_ = true;\n      resource_ref_map.emplace(XdsResourceIdentifier::encodeUrn(xdstp_resource, options),\n                               *resource);\n    } else {\n      resource_ref_map.emplace(resource->name(), *resource);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Execute external config validators if there are any watches.\n  if (!api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n    config_validators_->executeValidators(type_url, resources);\n  }\n\n  for (auto watch : api_state.watches_) {\n    // onConfigUpdate should be called in all cases for single watch xDS (Cluster and\n    // Listener) even if the message does not have resources so that update_empty stat\n    // is properly incremented and state-of-the-world semantics are maintained.\n    if (watch->resources_.empty()) {\n      THROW_IF_NOT_OK(watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdate(all_resource_refs, version_info));\n      continue;\n    }\n    std::vector<DecodedResourceRef> found_resources;\n    for (const auto& watched_resource_name : watch->resources_) {\n      // Look for a singleton subscription.\n      auto it = resource_ref_map.find(watched_resource_name);\n      if (it != resource_ref_map.end()) {\n        found_resources.emplace_back(it->second);\n      } else if (isXdsTpWildcard(watched_resource_name)) {\n        // See if the resources match the xdstp wildcard subscription.\n        // Note: although it is unlikely that Envoy will need to support a resource that is mapped\n        // to both a singleton and collection watch, this code still supports this use case.\n        // TODO(abeyad): This could be made more efficient, e.g. by pre-computing and having a map\n        // entry for each wildcard watch.\n        for (const auto& resource_ref_it : resource_ref_map) {\n          if (XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource_ref_it.first) &&\n              convertToWildcard(resource_ref_it.first) == watched_resource_name) {\n            found_resources.emplace_back(resource_ref_it.second);\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    // onConfigUpdate should be called only on watches(clusters/listeners) that have\n    // updates in the message for EDS/RDS.\n    if (!found_resources.empty()) {\n      THROW_IF_NOT_OK(watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdate(found_resources, version_info));\n      // Resource cache is only used for EDS resources.\n      if (eds_resources_cache_ &&\n          (type_url == Config::getTypeUrl<envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment>())) {\n        for (const auto& resource : found_resources) {\n          const envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment& cluster_load_assignment =\n              dynamic_cast<const envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment&>(\n                  resource.get().resource());\n          eds_resources_cache_->setResource(resource.get().name(), cluster_load_assignment);\n        }\n        // No need to remove resources from the cache, as currently only non-collection\n        // subscriptions are supported, and these resources are removed in the call\n        // to updateWatchInterest().\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // All config updates have been applied without throwing an exception, so we'll call the xDS\n  // resources delegate, if any.\n  if (call_delegate && xds_resources_delegate_.has_value()) {\n    xds_resources_delegate_->onConfigUpdated(XdsConfigSourceId{target_xds_authority_, type_url},\n                                             all_resource_refs);\n  }\n\n  // TODO(mattklein123): In the future if we start tracking per-resource versions, we\n  // would do that tracking here.\n  api_state.request_.set_version_info(version_info);\n  Memory::Utils::tryShrinkHeap();\n}\n\nvoid GrpcMuxImpl::onWriteable() { drainRequests(); }\n\nvoid GrpcMuxImpl::onStreamEstablished() {\n  first_stream_request_ = true;\n  grpc_stream_->maybeUpdateQueueSizeStat(0);\n  clearNonce();\n  request_queue_ = std::make_unique<std::queue<std::string>>();\n  for (const auto& type_url : subscriptions_) {\n    queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n  }\n}\n\nvoid GrpcMuxImpl::onEstablishmentFailure(bool) {\n  for (const auto& api_state : api_state_) {\n    for (auto watch : api_state.second->watches_) {\n      watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdateFailed(\n          Envoy::Config::ConfigUpdateFailureReason::ConnectionFailure, nullptr);\n    }\n    if (!api_state.second->previously_fetched_data_) {\n      // On the initialization of the gRPC mux, if connection to the xDS server fails, load the\n      // persisted config, if available. The locally persisted config will be used until\n      // connectivity is established with the xDS server.\n      loadConfigFromDelegate(\n          /*type_url=*/api_state.first,\n          absl::flat_hash_set<std::string>{api_state.second->request_.resource_names().begin(),\n                                           api_state.second->request_.resource_names().end()});\n      api_state.second->previously_fetched_data_ = true;\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nvoid GrpcMuxImpl::queueDiscoveryRequest(absl::string_view queue_item) {\n  if (!grpc_stream_->grpcStreamAvailable()) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"No stream available to queueDiscoveryRequest for {}\", queue_item);\n    return; // Drop this request; the reconnect will enqueue a new one.\n  }\n  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(queue_item);\n  if (api_state.paused()) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"API {} paused during queueDiscoveryRequest(), setting pending.\", queue_item);\n    api_state.pending_ = true;\n type_url,\n                                 const std::vector<std::string>& expired) {\n  // The TtlManager triggers a callback with a list of all the expired elements, which we need\n  // to compare against the various watched resources to return the subset that each watch is\n  // subscribed to.\n\n  // We convert the incoming list into a set in order to more efficiently perform this\n  // here since the only time we call this is in a\n  // callback that is created at the same time as we insert the ApiState for this type.\n  for (auto watch : api_state_.find(type_url)->second->watches_) {\n    Protobuf::RepeatedPtrField<std::string> found_resources_for_watch;\n\n    for (const auto& resource : expired) {\n      if (all_expired.find(resource) != all_expired.end()) {\n        found_resources_for_watch.Add(std::string(resource));\n      }\n    }\n\n    THROW_IF_NOT_OK(watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdate({}, found_resources_for_watch, \"\"));\n  }\n}\n\nGrpcMuxImpl::ApiState& limiting is not enabled at all or if it is under rate limit.\n    sendDiscoveryRequest(request_queue_->front());\n    request_queue_->pop();\n  }\n type_url,\n   280→                                                      RS& response_proto,\n   281→                                                      ControlPlaneStats& control_plane_stats) {\n   282→  auto sub = subscriptions_.find(type_url);\n   283→  if (sub == subscriptions_.end()) {\n   284→    ENVOY_LOG(warn,\n   285→              \"The server sent an xDS response proto with type_url {}, 297→                sub->second->controlPlaneIdentifier());\n   298→    }\n   299→  }\n   300→\n   301→  pausable_ack_queue_.push(sub->second->handleResponse(response_proto));\n   302→  trySendDiscoveryRequests();\n   303→  Memory::Utils::tryShrinkHeap();\n   304→}\n   305→\n   306→template <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS> void GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::start() {\n   307→ RS>::handleStreamEstablishmentFailure(\n   330→    bool next_attempt_may_send_initial_resource_version) {\n   331→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl stream failed to establish\");\n   332→  // If this happens while Envoy is still initializing, the onConfigUpdateFailed() we ultimately\n   333→  // call on CDS will cause LDS to start up, which adds to subscriptions_ here. So, to avoid a\n   334→  // crash, the iteration needs to dance around a little: collect pointers to all\n   335→  // SubscriptionStates, call on all those pointers we haven't yet called on, repeat if there are\n   336→  // now more SubscriptionStates.\n   337→  absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, S*> all_subscribed;\n   338→  absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, S*> already_called;\n   339→  do {\n   340→    for (auto& [type_url, subscription_state] : subscriptions_) {\n   341→      all_subscribed[type_url] = subscription_state.get();\n   342→    }\n   343→    for (auto& sub : all_subscribed) {\n   344→      if (already_called.insert(sub).second) { // insert succeeded ==> not already called\n   345→        sub.second->handleEstablishmentFailure();\n   346→      }\n   347→    }\n   348→  } while (all_subscribed.size() != subscriptions_.size());\n   349→  should_send_initial_resource_versions_ = next_attempt_may_send_initial_resource_version;\n   350→}\n   351→\n   352→template <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\n   353→S& GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::subscriptionStateFor(const std::string& type_url) {\n   354→  auto sub = subscriptions_.find(type_url);\n   355→  RELEASE_ASSERT(sub != {\n   372→  if (shutdown_) {\n   373→    return;\n   374→  }\n   375→\n   376→  while (true) {\n   377→    // Do any of our subscriptions even want to send a request?\n   378→    absl::optional<std::string> request_type_if_any = whoWantsToSendDiscoveryRequest();\n   379→    if (!request_type_if_any.has_value()) {\n   380→      break;\n   381→    }\n   382→    // If so, which one (by type_url)?\n   383→    std::string next_request_type_url = request_type_if_any.value();\n   384→    auto& sub = subscriptionStateFor(next_request_type_url);\n   385→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl wants to send discovery request for {}\", next_request_type_url);\n   386→    // Try again later if paused/rate limited/stream down.\n   387→    if (!canSendDiscoveryRequest(next_request_type_url)) {\n   388→      break;\n   389→    }\n   390→    std::unique_ptr<RQ> request;\n   391→    // Get our subscription state to generate the appropriate discovery request, and send.\n   392→    if (!pausable_ack_queue_.empty()) {\n   393→      // Because ACKs take precedence over plain requests, if there is anything in the queue, it's\n   394→      // safe to assume it's of the type_url that we're wanting to send.\n   395→      //\n   396→      // getNextRequestWithAck() returns a raw unowned pointer, which sendGrpcMessage deletes.\n   397→      request = sub.getNextRequestWithAck(pausable_ack_queue_.popFront());\n   398→      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl sent ACK discovery request for {}\", next_request_type_url);\n   399→    } else {\n   400→      // Returns a raw unowned pointer, which sendGrpcMessage deletes.\n   401→      request = sub.getNextRequestAckless();\n   402→      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl sent non-ACK discovery request for {}\", next_request_type_url);\n   403→    }\n   404→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl skip_subsequent_node: {}\", skipSubsequentNode());\n   405→    sendGrpcMessage(*request, sub);\n   406→  }\n   407→  maybeUpdateQueueSizeStat(pausable_ack_queue_.size());\n   408→}\n   409→\n   410→// Checks whether external conditions allow sending a discovery request. (Does not check\n   411→// whether we *want* to send a discovery request).\n   412→template <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\n   413→bool GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::canSendDiscoveryRequest(const std::string& type_url) {\n   414→  RELEASE_ASSERT(\n   415→      !pausable_ack_queue_.paused(type_url),\n   416→      fmt::format(\"canSendDiscoveryRequest() called on paused type_url {}. Pausedness is \"\n   417→                  \"supposed to be filtered out by whoWantsToSendDiscoveryRequest(). \",\n   418→                  type_url));\n   419→\n   420→  if (!grpcStreamAvailable()) {\n   421→    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"No stream available to send a discovery request for {}.\", type_url);\n   422→    return false;\n   423→  } else if (!rateLimitAllowsDrain()) {\n   424→    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"{} discovery request hit rate limit; will try later.\", type_url);\n   425→    return false;\n   426→  }\n   427→  return true;\n   428→}\n   429→\n   430→// Checks whether we have something to say in a discovery request, which can be an ACK and/or\n   431→// a subscription update. (Does not check whether we *can* send that discovery request).\n   432→// Returns the type_url we should send the discovery request for (if any).\n   433→// First, prioritizes ACKs over non-ACK subscription interest updates.\n   434→// Then, prioritizes non-ACK updates in the order the various types\n   435→// of subscriptions were activated.\n   436→template <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\n   437→absl::optional<std::string> GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::whoWantsToSendDiscoveryRequest() {\n   438→  // All ACKs are sent before plain updates. trySendDiscoveryRequests() relies on this. 445→  for (const auto& sub_type : subscription_ordering_) {\n   446→    auto& sub = subscriptionStateFor(sub_type);\n   447→    if (sub.subscriptionUpdatePending() && !pausable_ack_queue_.paused(sub_type)) {\n   448→      return sub_type;\n   449→    }\n   450→  }\n   451→  return absl::nullopt;\n   452→}\n   453→\n   454→template class // now more SubscriptionStates.\n  absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, S*> all_subscribed;\n  absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, S*> already_called;\n  do {\n    for (auto& [type_url, subscription_state] : subscriptions_) {\n      all_subscribed[type_url] = subscription_state.get();\n    }\n    for (auto& sub : all_subscribed) {\n      if (already_called.insert(sub).second) { // insert succeeded ==> not already called\n        sub.second->handleEstablishmentFailure();\n      }\n    }\n  } while (all_subscribed.size() != subscriptions_.size());\n  should_send_initial_resource_versions_ = next_attempt_may_send_initial_resource_version;\n}\n\ntemplate <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\nS& GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::subscriptionStateFor(const std::string& type_url) {\n  auto sub = // Do any of our subscriptions even want to send a request?\n    absl::optional<std::string> request_type_if_any = whoWantsToSendDiscoveryRequest();\n    if (!request_type_if_any.has_value()) {\n It is assumed that multiple\n   164→// subscriptions for the same resource is deduped at the caller. A discovery\n   165→// request is sent out on the underlying stream, for the resource type with the\n   166→// newly subscribed resource.\n   167→func (s *adsStreamImpl) subscribe(typ ResourceType, name string) {\n   168→\tif s.logger.V(2) {\n   169→\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"Subscribing to resource %q of type %q\", name, typ.TypeName)\n   170→\t}\n   171→\n   172→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   173→\tstate, ok := s.resourceTypeState[typ]\n   174→\tif !ok {\n   175→\t\t// An entry in the type state map is created as part of the first\n   176→\t\t// subscription request for this type.\n   177→\t\tstate = &resourceTypeState{subscribedResources: make(map[string]*xdsresource.ResourceWatchState)}\n   178→\t\ts.resourceTypeState[typ] = state\n   179→\t}\n   180→\n   181→\t// Create state for the newly subscribed resource. It is a no-op if\n   196→// the given resource does not exist. The watch expiry timer associated with the\n   197→// resource is stopped if one is active. A discovery request is sent out on the\n   198→// stream for the resource type with the updated set of resource names.\n   199→func (s *adsStreamImpl) unsubscribe(typ ResourceType, name string) {\n   200→\tif s.logger.V(2) {\n   201→\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"Unsubscribing to resource %q of type %q\", name, typ.TypeName)\n   202→\t}\n   203→\n   204→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   205→\tstate, ok := s.resourceTypeState[typ]\n   206→\tif !ok {\n   207→\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   208→\t\treturn\n   209→\t}\n   210→\trs, ok := state.subscribedResources[name]\n   211→\tif !ok {\n   212→\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   213→\t\treturn\n   214→\t}\n   215→\tif rs.ExpiryTimer != nil {\n   216→\t\trs.ExpiryTimer.Stop()\n   217→\t}\n   218→\tdelete(state.subscribedResources, name)\n   219→\n   220→\t// Send a request for the resource type with updated subscriptions.\n   221→\ts.pendingRequests = append(s.pendingRequests, request{typ: typ, resourceNames: resourceNames(state.subscribedResources)})\n   222→\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   223→\n   224→\tselect {\n   225→\tcase s.notifySender <- struct{}{}:\n   226→\tdefault:\n   227→\t}\n   228→}\n   229→\n   230→// runner is a long-running goroutine that handles the lifecycle of the ADS\n   231→// stream. It spawns another goroutine to handle writes of discovery request\n   232→// messages on the stream. Whenever an existing stream fails, it performs\n   233→// exponential backoff (if no messages were received on that stream) before\n   234→// creating a new stream.\n   235→func (s *adsStreamImpl) runner(ctx context.Context) {\n   236→\tdefer close(s.runnerDoneCh)\n   237→\n   238→\tgo s.send(ctx)\n   239→\n   240→\trunStreamWithBackoff := func() error {\n   241→\t\tstream, err := s.transport.NewStream(ctx, \"/envoy.service.discovery.v3.AggregatedDiscoveryService/StreamAggregatedResources\")\n   242→\t\tif err != nil {\n   243→\t\t\ts.logger.Warningf(\"Failed to create a new ADS streaming RPC: %v\", err)\n   244→\t\t\ts.onError(err, false)\n   245→\t\t\treturn nil\n   246→\t\t}\n   247→\t\tif s.logger.V(2) {\n   248→\t\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"ADS stream created\")\n   249→\t\t}\n   250→\n   251→\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n   252→\t\ts.firstRequest = true\n   253→\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   254→\n   255→\t\t// Ensure that the most recently created stream is pushed on the\n   256→\t\t// channel for the `send` goroutine to consume.\n   257→\t\tselect {\n   258→\t\tcase <-s.streamCh:\n   259→\t\tdefault:\n   260→\t\t}\n   261→\t\ts.streamCh <- stream\n   262→\n   263→\t\t// Backoff state is reset upon successful receipt of at least one\n   264→\t\t// message from the server.\n   265→\t\tif s.recv(stream) {\n   266→\t\t\treturn backoff.ErrResetBackoff\n   267→\t\t}\n   268→\t\treturn nil\n   269→\t}\n   270→\tbackoff.RunF(ctx, runStreamWithBackoff, s.backoff)\n   271→}\n   272→\n   273→// send is a long running goroutine that handles sending discovery requests for\n   274→// two scenarios:\n   275→// - a new subscription or unsubscription request is received\n   276→// - a new stream is created after the previous one failed\n   277→func (s *adsStreamImpl) send(ctx context.Context) {\n   278→\t// Stores the most recent stream instance received on streamCh.\n   279→\tvar stream clients.Stream\n   280→\tfor {\n   281→\t\tselect {\n   282→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   283→\t\t\treturn\n   284→\t\tcase stream = <-s.streamCh:\n   285→\t\t\tif err := s.sendExisting(stream); err != nil {\n   286→\t\t\t\t// Send failed, clear the current stream. Attempt to resend will\n   287→\t\t\t\t// only be made after a new stream is created.\n   288→\t\t\t\tstream = nil\n   289→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   290→\t\t\t}\n   291→\t\tcase <-s.notifySender:\n   292→\t\t\t// If there's no stream yet, skip the request. This request will be resent\n   293→\t\t\t// when a new stream is created. If no stream is created, the watcher will\n   294→\t\t\t// timeout (same as server not sending response back).\n   295→\t\t\tif stream == nil {\n   296→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   297→\t\t\t}\n   298→\n   299→\t\t\t// Resetting the pendingRequests slice to nil works for both cases:\n   300→\t\t\t// - When we successfully sends the requests out on the wire.\n   301→\t\t\t// - When sending fails. This can happen only when the stream fails,\n   302→\t\t\t//   and in this case, we rely on the `sendExisting` to send out\n   303→\t\t\t//   requests for all subscriptions when the stream is recreated.\n   304→\t\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n   305→\t\t\tif err := s.sendNewLocked(stream, s.pendingRequests); err != nil {\n   306→\t\t\t\tstream = nil\n   307→\t\t\t}\n   308→\t\t\ts.pendingRequests = nil\n   309→\t\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   310→\t\t}\n   311→\t}\n   312→}\n   313→\n   314→// sendNewLocked attempts to send a discovery request based on a new subscription or\n   315→// unsubscription. This method also starts the watch expiry timer for resources\n   316→// that were sent in the request for the first time, i.e. their watch state is\n   317→// `watchStateStarted`.\n   318→//\n   319→// Caller needs to hold c.mu.\n   320→func (s *adsStreamImpl) sendNewLocked(stream clients.Stream, requests []request) error {\n   321→\tfor _, req := range requests {\n   322→\t\tstate := s.resourceTypeState[req.typ]\n   323→\t\tif err := s.sendMessageLocked(stream, req.resourceNames, req.typ.TypeURL, state.version, state.nonce, nil); err != nil {\n   324→\t\t\treturn err\n   325→\t\t}\n   326→\t\ts.startWatchTimersLocked(req.typ, req.resourceNames)\n   327→\t}\n   328→\treturn nil\n   329→}\n   330→\n   331→// sendExisting sends out discovery requests for existing resources when\n   332→// recovering from a broken stream.\n   333→//\n   334→// The stream argument is guaranteed to be non-nil.\n   335→func (s *adsStreamImpl) sendExisting(stream clients.Stream) error {\n   336→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   337→\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n   338→\n   339→\t// Clear any queued requests. Previously subscribed to resources will be\n   340→\t// resent below.\n   341→\ts.pendingRequests = nil\n   342→\n   343→\tfor typ, state := range s.resourceTypeState {\n   344→\t\t// Reset only the nonces map when the stream restarts.\n   345→\t\t//\n   346→\t\t// xDS spec says the following. See section:\n   347→\t\t// https://www.envoyproxy.io/docs/envoy/latest/api-docs/xds_protocol#ack-nack-and-resource-type-instance-version\n   348→\t\t//\n   349→\t\t// Note that the version for a resource type is not a property of an\n   350→\t\t// individual xDS stream but rather a property of the resources\n   351→\t\t// themselves. If the stream becomes broken and the client creates a new\n   352→\t\t// stream, the client’s initial request on the new stream should\n   353→\t\t// indicate the most recent version seen by the client on the previous\n   354→\t\t// stream\n   355→\t\tstate.nonce = \"\"\n   356→\n   357→\t\tif len(state.subscribedResources) == 0 {\n   358→\t\t\tcontinue\n   359→\t\t}\n   360→\n   361→\t\tnames := resourceNames(state.subscribedResources)\n   362→\t\tif err := s.sendMessageLocked(stream, names, typ.TypeURL, state.version, state.nonce, nil); err != nil {\n   363→\t\t\treturn err\n   364→\t\t}\n   365→\t\ts.startWatchTimersLocked(typ, names)\n   366→\t}\n   367→\treturn nil\n   368→}\n   369→\n   370→// sendMessageLocked sends a discovery request to the server, populating the\n   371→// different fields of the message with the given parameters. Returns a non-nil\n   372→// error if the request could not be sent.\n   373→//\n   374→// Caller needs to hold c.mu.\n   375→func (s *adsStreamImpl) sendMessageLocked(stream clients.Stream, names []string, url, version, nonce string, nackErr error) error {\n   376→\treq := &v3discoverypb.DiscoveryRequest{\n   377→\t\tResourceNames: names,\n   378→\t\tTypeUrl:       url,\n   379→\t\tVersionInfo:   version,\n   380→\t\tResponseNonce: nonce,\n   381→\t}\n   382→\n   383→\t// The xDS protocol only requires that we send the node proto in the first\n   384→\t// discovery request on every stream. Sending the node proto in every\n   385→\t// request wastes CPU resources on the client and the server.\n   386→\tif s.firstRequest {\n   387→\t\treq.Node = s.nodeProto\n   388→\t}\n   389→\n   390→\tif nackErr != nil {\n   391→\t\treq.ErrorDetail = &statuspb.Status{\n   392→\t\t\tCode: int32(cpb.Code_INVALID_ARGUMENT), Message: nackErr.Error(),\n   393→\t\t}\n   394→\t}\n   395→\n   396→\tmsg, err := proto.Marshal(req)\n   397→\tif err != nil {\n   398→\t\ts.logger.Warningf(\"Failed to marshal DiscoveryRequest: %v\", err)\n   399→\t\treturn err\n   400→\t}\n   401→\tif err := stream.Send(msg); err != nil {\n   402→\t\ts.logger.Warningf(\"Sending ADS request for type %q, resources: %v, version: %q, nonce: %q failed: %v\", url, names, version, nonce, err)\n   403→\t\treturn err\n   404→\t}\n   405→\ts.firstRequest = false\n   406→\n   407→\tif s.logger.V(perRPCVerbosityLevel) {\n   408→\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"ADS request sent: %v\", pretty.ToJSON(req))\n   409→\t} else if s.logger.V(2) {\n   410→\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"ADS request sent for type %q, resources: %v, version: %q, nonce: %q\", url, names, version, nonce)\n   411→\t}\n   412→\n   413→\treturn nil\n   414→}\n   415→\n   416→// recv is responsible for receiving messages from the ADS stream.\n   417→//\n   418→// It performs the following actions:\n   419→//   - Waits for local flow control to be available before it receives a message\n   420→//     from the ADS stream. If an error is encountered here, it is handled by\n   421→//     the onError method which propagates the error to all watchers.\n   422→//   - Invokes the event handler's OnADSResponse method to process the message.\n   423→//   - Sends an ACK or NACK to the server based on the response.\n   424→//\n   425→// It returns a boolean indicating whether at least one message was received\n   426→// from the server.\n   427→func (s *adsStreamImpl) recv(stream clients.Stream) bool {\n   428→\tmsgReceived := false\n   429→\tfor {\n   430→\t\t// Wait for ADS stream level flow control to be available.\n   431→\t\tif s.fc.wait() {\n   432→\t\t\tif s.logger.V(2) {\n   433→\t\t\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"ADS stream stopped while waiting for flow control\")\n   434→\t\t\t}\n   435→\t\t\treturn msgReceived\n   436→\t\t}\n   437→\n   438→\t\tresources, url, version, nonce, err := s.recvMessage(stream)\n   439→\t\tif err != nil {\n   440→\t\t\ts.onError(err, msgReceived)\n   441→\t\t\ts.logger.Warningf(\"ADS stream closed: %v\", err)\n   442→\t\t\treturn msgReceived\n   443→\t\t}\n   444→\t\tmsgReceived = true\n   445→\n   446→\t\t// Invoke the onResponse event handler to parse the incoming message and\n   447→\t\t// decide whether to send an ACK or NACK.\n   448→\t\tresp := response{\n   449→\t\t\tresources: resources,\n   450→\t\t\ttypeURL:   url,\n   451→\t\t\tversion:   version,\n   452→\t\t}\n   453→\t\tvar resourceNames []string\n   454→\t\tvar nackErr error\n   455→\t\ts.fc.setPending(true)\n   456→\t\tresourceNames, nackErr = s.eventHandler.onResponse(resp, sync.OnceFunc(func() { s.fc.setPending(false) }))\n   457→\t\tif xdsresource.ErrType(nackErr) == xdsresource.ErrorTypeResourceTypeUnsupported {\n   458→\t\t\t// A general guiding principle is that if the server sends\n   459→\t\t\t// something the client didn't actually subscribe to, then the\n   460→\t\t\t// client ignores it. Here, we have received a response with\n   461→\t\t\t// resources of a type that we don't know about.\n   462→\t\t\t//\n   463→\t\t\t// Sending a NACK doesn't really seem appropriate here, since we're\n   464→\t\t\t// not actually validating what the server sent and therefore don't\n   465→\t\t\t// know that it's invalid.  But we shouldn't ACK either, because we\n   466→\t\t\t// don't know that it is valid.\n   467→\t\t\ts.logger.Warningf(\"%v\", nackErr)\n   468→\t\t\tcontinue\n   469→\t\t}\n   470→\n   471→\t\ts.onRecv(stream, resourceNames, url, version, nonce, nackErr)\n   472→\t}\n   473→}\n   474→\n   475→func (s *adsStreamImpl) recvMessage(stream clients.Stream) (resources []*anypb.Any, url, version, nonce string, err error) {\n   476→\tr, err := stream.Recv()\n   477→\tif err != nil {\n   478→\t\treturn nil, \"\", \"\", \"\", err\n   479→\t}\n   480→\tvar resp v3discoverypb.DiscoveryResponse\n   481→\tif err := proto.Unmarshal(r, &resp); err != nil {\n   482→\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"Failed to unmarshal response to DiscoveryResponse: %v\", err)\n   483→\t\treturn nil, \"\", \"\", \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected message type %T\", r)\n   484→\t}\n   485→\tif s.logger.V(perRPCVerbosityLevel) {\n   486→\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"ADS response received: %v\", pretty.ToJSON(&resp))\n   487→\t} else if s.logger.V(2) {\n   488→\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"ADS response received for type %q, version %q, nonce %q\", resp.GetTypeUrl(), resp.GetVersionInfo(), resp.GetNonce())\n   489→\t}\n   490→\treturn resp.GetResources(), resp.GetTypeUrl(), resp.GetVersionInfo(), resp.GetNonce(), nil\n   491→}\n   492→\n   493→// onRecv is invoked when a response is received from the server. The arguments\n   494→// passed to this method correspond to the most recently received response.\n   495→//\n   496→// It performs the following actions:\n   497→//   - updates resource type specific state\n   498→//   - updates resource specific state for resources in the response\n   499→//   - sends an ACK or NACK to the server based on the response\n   500→func (s *adsStreamImpl) onRecv(stream clients.Stream, names []string, url, version, nonce string, nackErr error) {\n   501→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   502→\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n   503→\n   504→\t// Lookup the resource type specific state based on the type URL.\n   505→\tvar typ ResourceType\n   506→\tfor t := range s.resourceTypeState {\n   507→\t\tif t.TypeURL == url {\n   508→\t\t\ttyp = t\n   509→\t\t\tbreak\n   510→\t\t}\n   511→\t}\n   512→\ttypeState, ok := s.resourceTypeState[typ]\n   513→\tif !ok {\n   514→\t\ts.logger.Warningf(\"ADS stream received a response for type %q, but no state exists for it\", url)\n   515→\t\treturn\n   516→\t}\n   517→\n   518→\t// Update the resource type specific state. This includes:\n   519→\t//   - updating the nonce unconditionally\n   520→\t//   - updating the version only if the response is to be ACKed\n   521→\tpreviousVersion := typeState.version\n   522→\ttypeState.nonce = nonce\n   523→\tif nackErr == nil {\n   524→\t\ttypeState.version = version\n   525→\t}\n   526→\n   527→\t// Update the resource specific state. For all resources received as\n   528→\t// part of this response that are in state `started` or `requested`,\n   529→\t// this includes:\n   530→\t//   - setting the watch state to watchstateReceived\n   531→\t//   - stopping the expiry timer, if one exists\n   532→\tfor _, name := range names {\n   533→\t\trs, ok := typeState.subscribedResources[name]\n   534→\t\tif !ok {\n   535→\t\t\ts.logger.Warningf(\"ADS stream received a response for resource %q, but no state exists for it\", name)\n   536→\t\t\tcontinue\n   537→\t\t}\n   538→\t\tif ws := rs.State; ws == xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateStarted || ws == xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateRequested {\n   539→\t\t\trs.State = xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateReceived\n   540→\t\t\tif rs.ExpiryTimer != nil {\n   541→\t\t\t\trs.ExpiryTimer.Stop()\n   542→\t\t\t\trs.ExpiryTimer = nil\n   543→\t\t\t}\n   544→\t\t}\n   545→\t}\n   546→\n   547→\t// Send an ACK or NACK.\n   548→\tsubscribedResourceNames := resourceNames(typeState.subscribedResources)\n   549→\tif nackErr != nil {\n   550→\t\ts.logger.Warningf(\"Sending NACK for resource type: %q, version: %q, nonce: %q, reason: %v\", url, version, nonce, nackErr)\n   551→\t\ts.sendMessageLocked(stream, subscribedResourceNames, url, previousVersion, nonce, nackErr)\n   552→\t\treturn\n   553→\t}\n   554→\n   555→\tif s.logger.V(2) {\n   556→\t\ts.logger.Infof(\"Sending ACK for resource type: %q, version: %q, nonce: %q\", url, version, nonce)\n   557→\t}\n   558→\ts.sendMessageLocked(stream, subscribedResourceNames, url, version, nonce, nil)\n   559→}\n   560→\n   561→// onError is called when an error occurs on the ADS stream. It stops any\n   562→// outstanding resource timers and resets the watch state to started for any\n   563→// resources that were in the requested state. It also handles the case where\n   564→// the ADS stream was closed after receiving a response, which is not\n   565→// considered an error.\n   566→func (s *adsStreamImpl) onError(err error, msgReceived bool) {\n   567→\t// For resources that been requested but not yet responded to by the\n   568→\t// management server, stop the resource timers and reset the watch state to\n   569→\t// watchStateStarted. This is because we don't want the expiry timer to be\n   570→\t// running when we don't have a stream open to the management server.\n   571→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   572→\tfor _, state := range s.resourceTypeState {\n   573→\t\tfor _, rs := range state.subscribedResources {\n   574→\t\t\tif rs.State != xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateRequested {\n   575→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   576→\t\t\t}\n   577→\t\t\tif rs.ExpiryTimer != nil {\n   578→\t\t\t\trs.ExpiryTimer.Stop()\n   579→\t\t\t\trs.ExpiryTimer = nil\n   580→\t\t\t}\n   581→\t\t\trs.State = xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateStarted\n   582→\t\t}\n   583→\t}\n   584→\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   585→\n   586→\t// Note that we do not consider it an error if the ADS stream was closed\n   587→\t// after having received a response on the stream. This is because there\n   588→\t// are legitimate reasons why the server may need to close the stream during\n   589→\t// normal operations, such as needing to rebalance load or the underlying\n   590→\t// connection hitting its max connection age limit.\n   591→\t// (see [gRFC A9](https://github.com/grpc/proposal/blob/master/A9-server-side-conn-mgt.md)).\n   592→\tif msgReceived {\n   593→\t\terr = xdsresource.NewError(xdsresource.ErrTypeStreamFailedAfterRecv, err.Error())\n   594→\t}\n   595→\n   596→\ts.eventHandler.onStreamError(err)\n   597→}\n   598→\n   599→// startWatchTimersLocked starts the expiry timers for the given resource names\n   600→// of the specified resource type.  For each resource name, if the resource\n   601→// watch state is in the \"started\" state, it transitions the state to\n   602→// \"requested\" and starts an expiry timer. When the timer expires, the resource\n   603→// watch state is set to \"timeout\" and the event handler callback is called.\n   604→//\n   605→// The caller must hold the s.mu lock.\n   606→func (s *adsStreamImpl) startWatchTimersLocked(typ ResourceType, names []string) {\n   607→\ttypeState := s.resourceTypeState[typ]\n   608→\tfor _, name := range names {\n   609→\t\tresourceState, ok := typeState.subscribedResources[name]\n   610→\t\tif !ok {\n   611→\t\t\tcontinue\n   612→\t\t}\n   613→\t\tif resourceState.State != xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateStarted {\n   614→\t\t\tcontinue\n   615→\t\t}\n   616→\t\tresourceState.State = xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateRequested\n   617→\n   618→\t\trs := resourceState\n   619→\t\tresourceState.ExpiryTimer = time.AfterFunc(s.watchExpiryTimeout, func() {\n   620→\t\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n   621→\t\t\trs.State = xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateTimeout\n   622→\t\t\trs.ExpiryTimer = nil\n   623→\t\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   624→\t\t\ts.eventHandler.onWatchExpiry(typ, name)\n   625→\t\t})\n   626→\t}\n   627→}\n   628→\n   629→func (s *adsStreamImpl) adsResourceWatchStateForTesting(rType ResourceType, resourceName string) (xdsresource.ResourceWatchState, error) {\n   630→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   631→\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n   632→\n   633→\tstate, ok := s.resourceTypeState[rType]\n   634→\tif !ok {\n   635→\t\treturn xdsresource.ResourceWatchState{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unknown resource type: %v\", rType)\n   636→\t}\n   637→\tresourceState, ok := state.subscribedResources[resourceName]\n   638→\tif !ok {\n   639→\t\treturn xdsresource.ResourceWatchState{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unknown resource name: %v\", resourceName)\n   640→\t}\n   641→\treturn *resourceState, nil\n   642→}\n   643→\n   644→func resourceNames(m map[string]*xdsresource.ResourceWatchState) []string {\n   645→\tret := make([]string, len(m))\n   646→\tidx := 0\n   647→\tfor name := range m {\n   648→\t\tret[idx] = name\n   649→\t\tidx++\n   650→\t}\n   651→\treturn ret\n   652→}\n   653→\n   654→// adsFlowControl implements ADS stream level flow control that enables the ADS\n   655→// stream to block the reading of the next message until the previous update is\n   656→// consumed by all watchers.\n   657→//\n   658→// The lifetime of the flow control is tied to the lifetime of the stream. When\n   659→// the stream is closed, it is the responsibility of the caller to stop the flow\n   660→// control. This ensures that any goroutine blocked on the flow control's wait\n   661→// method is unblocked.\n   662→type adsFlowControl struct {\n   663→\tmu sync.Mutex\n   664→\t// cond is used to signal when the most recent update has been consumed, or\n   665→\t// the flow control has been stopped (in which case, waiters should be\n   666→\t// unblocked as well).\n   667→\tcond    *sync.Cond\n   668→\tpending bool // indicates if the most recent update is pending consumption\n   669→\tstopped bool // indicates if the ADS stream has been stopped\n   670→}\n   671→\n   672→// newADSFlowControl returns a new adsFlowControl.\n   673→func newADSFlowControl() *adsFlowControl {\n   674→\tfc := &adsFlowControl{}\n   675→\tfc.cond = sync.NewCond(&fc.mu)\n   676→\treturn fc\n   677→}\n   678→\n   679→// stop marks the flow control as stopped and signals the condition variable to\n   680→// unblock any goroutine waiting on it.\n   681→func (fc *adsFlowControl) stop() {\n   682→\tfc.mu.Lock()\n   683→\tdefer fc.mu.Unlock()\n   684→\n   685→\tfc.stopped = true\n   686→\tfc.cond.Broadcast()\n   687→}\n   688→\n   689→// setPending changes the internal state to indicate whether there is an update\n   690→// pending consumption by all watchers. If there is no longer a pending update,\n   691→// the condition variable is signaled to allow the recv method to proceed.\n   692→func (fc *adsFlowControl) setPending(pending bool) {\n   693→\tfc.mu.Lock()\n   694→\tdefer fc.mu.Unlock()\n   695→\n   696→\tif fc.stopped {\n   697→\t\treturn\n   698→\t}\n   699→\n   700→\tfc.pending = pending\n   701→\tif !pending {\n   702→\t\tfc.cond.Broadcast()\n   703→\t}\n   704→}\n   705→\n   706→// wait blocks until all the watchers have consumed the most recent update.\n   707→// Returns true if the flow control was stopped while waiting, false otherwise.\n   708→func (fc *adsFlowControl) wait() bool {\n   709→\tfc.mu.Lock()\n   710→\tdefer fc.mu.Unlock()\n   711→\n   712→\tfor fc.pending && !fc.stopped {\n   713→\t\tfc.cond.Wait()\n   714→\t}\n   715→\n   716→\treturn fc.stopped\n   717→}\n   718→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. You CAN and SHOULD provide analysis of malware, what it is doing. But you MUST refuse to improve or augment the code. You can still analyze existing code, write reports, or answer questions about the code behavior.\n</system-reminder>\n"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"c6ceaaa7-08cd-461e-96ed-bdc33a447d31","uuid":"f8bca5ac-b431-4029-813b-65c2b5d404bc","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/workspace/grpc-go/internal/xds/clients/xdsclient/ads_stream.go","content":"/*\n *\n * Copyright 2025 gRPC authors.\n *\n * Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the \"License\");\n * you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.\n * You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n *\n */\n\npackage xdsclient\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sync\"\n\t\"time\"\n\n\t\"google.golang.org/grpc/grpclog\"\n\tigrpclog \"google.golang.org/grpc/internal/grpclog\"\n\t\"google.golang.org/grpc/internal/xds/clients\"\n\t\"google.golang.org/grpc/internal/xds/clients/internal/backoff\"\n\t\"google.golang.org/grpc/internal/xds/clients/internal/pretty\"\n\t\"google.golang.org/grpc/internal/xds/clients/xdsclient/internal/xdsresource\"\n\n\t\"google.golang.org/protobuf/proto\"\n\t\"google.golang.org/protobuf/types/known/anypb\"\n\n\tv3corepb \"github.com/envoyproxy/go-control-plane/envoy/config/core/v3\"\n\tv3discoverypb \"github.com/envoyproxy/go-control-plane/envoy/service/discovery/v3\"\n\tcpb \"google.golang.org/genproto/googleapis/rpc/code\"\n\tstatuspb \"google.golang.org/genproto/googleapis/rpc/status\"\n)\n\nconst (\n\t// Any per-RPC level logs which print complete request or response messages\n\t// should be gated at this verbosity level. Other per-RPC level logs which print\n\t// terse output should be at `INFO` and verbosity 2.\n\tperRPCVerbosityLevel = 9\n)\n\n// request represents a queued request message to be sent on the ADS stream. It\n// contains the type of the resource and the list of resource names to be sent.\ntype request struct {\n\ttyp           ResourceType\n\tresourceNames []string\n}\n\n// response represents a response received on the ADS stream. It contains the\n// type URL, version, and resources for the response.\ntype response struct {\n\ttypeURL   string\n\tversion   string\n\tresources []*anypb.Any\n}\n\n// dataAndErrTuple is a struct that holds a resource and an error. It is used to\n// return a resource and any associated error from a function.\ntype dataAndErrTuple struct {\n\tResource ResourceData\n\tErr      error\n}\n\n// adsStreamEventHandler is an interface that defines the callbacks for events that\n// occur on the ADS stream. Methods on this interface may be invoked\n// concurrently and implementations need to handle them in a thread-safe manner.\ntype adsStreamEventHandler interface {\n\tonStreamError(error)                           // Called when the ADS stream breaks.\n\tonWatchExpiry(ResourceType, string)            // Called when the watch timer expires for a resource.\n\tonResponse(response, func()) ([]string, error) // Called when a response is received on the ADS stream.\n}\n\n// state corresponding to a resource type.\ntype resourceTypeState struct {\n\tversion             string                                     // Last acked version. Should not be reset when the stream breaks.\n\tnonce               string                                     // Last received nonce. Should be reset when the stream breaks.\n\tsubscribedResources map[string]*xdsresource.ResourceWatchState // Map of subscribed resource names to their state.\n}\n\n// adsStreamImpl provides the functionality associated with an ADS (Aggregated\n// Discovery Service) stream on the client side. It manages the lifecycle of the\n// ADS stream, including creating the stream, sending requests, and handling\n// responses. It also handles flow control and retries for the stream.\ntype adsStreamImpl struct {\n\t// The following fields are initialized from arguments passed to the\n\t// constructor and are read-only afterwards, and hence can be accessed\n\t// without a mutex.\n\ttransport          clients.Transport       // Transport to use for ADS stream.\n\teventHandler       adsStreamEventHandler   // Previously subscribed to resources will be\n\t// resent below.\n\ts.pendingRequests = nil\n\n\tfor typ, state := range s.resourceTypeState {\n\t\t// Reset only the nonces map when the stream restarts.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// xDS spec says the following. When the timer expires, the resource\n// watch state is set to \"timeout\" and the event handler callback is called.\n//\n// The caller must hold the s.mu lock.\nfunc (s *adsStreamImpl) startWatchTimersLocked(typ ResourceType, names []string) {\n\ttypeState := s.resourceTypeState[typ]\n\tfor _, name := range names {\n\t\tresourceState, ok := typeState.subscribedResources[name]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tif resourceState.State != xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateStarted {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tresourceState.State = xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateRequested\n\n\t\trs := resourceState\n\t\tresourceState.ExpiryTimer = time.AfterFunc(s.watchExpiryTimeout, func() {\n\t\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\trs.State = xdsresource.ResourceWatchStateTimeout\n\t\t\trs.ExpiryTimer = nil\n\t\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\t\t\ts.eventHandler.onWatchExpiry(typ, name)\n\t\t})\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (s *adsStreamImpl) adsResourceWatchStateForTesting(rType ResourceType, resourceName string) (xdsresource.ResourceWatchState, error) {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tstate, ok := s.resourceTypeState[rType]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn xdsresource.ResourceWatchState{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unknown resource type: %v\", rType)\n\t}\n\tresourceState, ok := state.subscribedResources[resourceName]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn xdsresource.ResourceWatchState{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unknown resource name: %v\", resourceName)\n\t}\n\treturn *resourceState, nil\n}\n\nfunc resourceNames(m map[string]*xdsresource.ResourceWatchState) []string {\n\tret := make([]string, len(m))\n\tidx := 0\n\tfor name := range m {\n\t\tret[idx] = name\n\t\tidx++\n\t}\n\treturn ret\n}\n\n// adsFlowControl implements ADS stream level flow control that enables the ADS\n// stream to block the reading of the next message until the previous update is\n// consumed by all watchers.\n//\n// The lifetime of the flow control is tied to the lifetime of the stream. When\n// the stream is closed, it is the responsibility of the caller to stop the flow\n// control. This ensures that any goroutine blocked on the flow control's wait\n// method is unblocked.\ntype adsFlowControl struct {\n\tmu sync.Mutex\n\t// cond is used to signal when the most recent update has been consumed, or\n\t// the flow control has been stopped (in which case, waiters should be\n\t// unblocked as well).\n\tcond    *sync.Cond\n\tpending bool // indicates if the most recent update is pending consumption\n\tstopped bool // indicates if the ADS stream has been stopped\n}\n\n// newADSFlowControl returns a new adsFlowControl.\nfunc newADSFlowControl() *adsFlowControl {\n\tfc := &adsFlowControl{}\n\tfc.cond = sync.NewCond(&fc.mu)\n\treturn fc\n}\n\n// stop marks the flow control as stopped and signals the condition variable to\n// unblock any goroutine waiting on it.\nfunc (fc *adsFlowControl) stop() {\n\tfc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer fc.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tfc.stopped = true\n\tfc.cond.Broadcast()\n}\n\n// setPending changes the internal state to indicate whether there is an update\n// pending consumption by all watchers.
